# This file, metarStationInfo.txt, contains station information for METAR and
# SAO sites. (Some Canadian station still report in SA format. Although these
# are now converted at OSO to METAR form, we note them as SAO here.)
#
# Good sources of station information include
# NWS/O0S:  http://www.nws.noaa.gov/tg/siteloc.shtml
# FAA ASOS: http://www.faa.gov/asos/asos.htm
# Unidata:  http://www.unidata.ucar.edu/staff/chiz/stations/stations.shtml
# AFWA:     ftp://ncardata.ucar.edu/datasets/ds900.0/data_1999.01
# AirNav, linked to the Unidata site, is excellent for U.S. sites.
# AES Canada has provided metadata on their stations. As much as possible,
# this file has been updated to reflect that information.
# There is now a Web site from which the data are available:
#           http://www.cmc.ec.gc.ca/climate/doc/metstat/
#
# Although most present geographic info carries a precision of .01 degree,
# space is available for an additional digit. As Jim Ramer points out, at
# maximum zoom on the WFO scale, .01 degree is about 30 pixels.
#
# Elevations are in meters. "-0" is used to signify unknown elevation.
#
# Stations marked "e" at the right include guesses for some of the information.
# In some cases, this is the lat/lon/elev, given a name, while in others, it's
# the station name, when we know ID & location.
#
# ID     lat      lon    elev           station name            country
#(5)  (sn2.3) (sn3.3)    (5)               (36)                  (2)
